Dravidian Etymological Dictionary(DED), 2nd

Edn. 1984, item No. 1793 Tamil: kuruvi, KurîI small

bird. Malayalam: kuruvi, kurikil, kûri sparrow. Kurub.

(LSB 1.12) kibbi id. Kannada: gubbi, gubbil, gubbacci

a small bird, esp. a sparrow. Tulu: gurubi, gurbi, gubbi

sparrow.
